DELIMITER $$
--
-- Procédures
--
CREATE DEFINER=`urzawebf`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `noteglobal` (IN `p_candidat` INT, IN `p_categorie` INT)  BEGIN
	SELECT SUM(note1), SUM(note2) FROM notecritere WHERE id_candidat=p_candidat AND id_categorie=p_categorie;
END$$

CREATE DEFINER=`urzawebf`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `notepoint` (IN `p_candidat` INT, IN `p_categorie` INT)  BEGIN
SELECT CONCAT('Point ',CC.point) AS point, SUM(AA.note1) AS note1, SUM(BB.ptse1) AS pts1, SUM(AA.note2) AS note2, SUM(BB.ptse2) AS pts2 FROM notecritere AS AA
	INNER JOIN critere AS BB ON BB.id = AA.id_critere
	INNER JOIN consigne AS CC ON CC.id = BB.id_consigne
	WHERE id_candidat=p_candidat AND id_categorie=p_categorie 
	GROUP BY CC.point;
END$$

CREATE DEFINER=`urzawebf`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `notetheme` (IN `p_candidat` INT, IN `p_categorie` INT)  BEGIN
	SELECT DD.label, SUM(AA.note1) AS note1, DD.pts1, SUM(AA.note2) AS note2, DD.pts2 FROM notecritere AS AA
	INNER JOIN critere AS BB ON BB.id = AA.id_critere
	INNER JOIN consigne AS CC ON CC.id = BB.id_consigne
	INNER JOIN theme AS DD ON DD.id = CC.id_theme
	WHERE AA.id_candidat=p_candidat AND AA.id_categorie=p_categorie 
	GROUP BY CC.id_theme;
END$$

DELIMITER ;

--
-- Déclencheurs `dossier`
--
DELIMITER $$
CREATE TRIGGER `create_num_dossier` BEFORE INSERT ON `dossier` FOR EACH ROW BEGIN
	DECLARE ValeurMax INTEGER;
	SELECT auto_increment INTO ValeurMax FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'urzawebf_test' AND table_name='dossier';
	#SELECT MAX(dossier.id)+1 INTO ValeurMax FROM dossier;
	SET NEW.num_dossier=concat('D',ValeurMax,'-',NEW.codeagence);
	#SET NEW.num_dossier = concat('D',NEW.id,'-',NEW.codeagence);
END
$$
DELIMITER ;

  `id_candidat` int(11) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

-- Structure de la table `presence`
--

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

  `_name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,

  `login` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `_password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,

  `email` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `codeagence` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 78
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COMMENT='Table utilisateurs';
